Insight Public Sector, Inc. Service Hourly Rates 
Insight’s digital security services empower businesses to protect their data, infrastructure, and 
users from evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity 
solutions, including risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.  
 
Their cybersecurity consulting team works closely with clients to build resilient security strategies 
tailored to specific risks and compliance needs, enabling companies to proactively address 
vulnerabilities. Insight’s services also encompass cloud security and endpoint protection, ensuring 
that data and devices remain secure across all digital environments.  
 
By integrating these solutions with advanced threat intelligence, Insight helps businesses stay 
ahead of cyberattacks while ensuring compliance and maintaining operational efficiency

evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity solutions, including 
risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.

Insight Public Sector, Inc. Service Hourly Rates 
Insight’s digital security services empower businesses to protect their data, infrastructure, and 
users from evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity 
solutions, including risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.

vulnerabilities. Insight’s services also encompass cloud security and endpoint protection, ensuring 
that data and devices remain secure across all digital environments.

ahead of cyberattacks while ensuring compliance and maintaining operational efficiency

Insight Public Sector, Inc. Service Hourly Rates 
Insight’s digital security services empower businesses to protect their data, infrastructure, and 
users from evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity 
solutions, including risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.  
 
Their cybersecurity consulting team works closely with clients to build resilient security strategies 
tailored to specific risks and compliance needs, enabling companies to proactively address 
vulnerabilities. Insight’s services also encompass cloud security and endpoint protection, ensuring 
that data and devices remain secure across all digital environments.

## Page 320

43230000-24-STC 
 
 Page 13 of 13 
Digital Security Solutions 
Insight’s digital security services empower businesses to protect their data, infrastructure, and 
users from evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity 
solutions, including risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.  
 
Their cybersecurity consulting team works closely with clients to build resilient security strategies 
tailored to specific risks and compliance needs, enabling companies to proactively address 
vulnerabilities. Insight’s services also encompass cloud security and endpoint protection, ensuring 
that data and devices remain secure across all digital environments.  
 
By integrating these solutions with advanced threat intelligence, Insight helps businesses stay 
ahead of cyberattacks while ensuring compliance and maintaining operational efficiency

Insight Public Sector, Inc. Service Hourly Rates 
Insight’s digital security services empower businesses to protect their data, infrastructure, and 
users from evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity 
solutions, including risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.  
 
Their cybersecurity consulting team works closely with clients to build resilient security strategies 
tailored to specific risks and compliance needs, enabling companies to proactively address 
vulnerabilities. Insight’s services also encompass cloud security and endpoint protection, ensuring 
that data and devices remain secure across all digital environments.  
 
By integrating these solutions with advanced threat intelligence, Insight helps businesses stay 
ahead of cyberattacks while ensuring compliance and maintaining operational efficiency   
Docusign Envelope ID: 58539CBB-F506-4DB1-BD17-4700815DDB34

Insight Public Sector, Inc. Service Hourly Rates 
Insight’s digital security services empower businesses to protect their data, infrastructure, and 
users from evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity 
solutions, including risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.  
 
Their cybersecurity consulting team works closely with clients to build resilient security strategies 
tailored to specific risks and compliance needs, enabling companies to proactively address 
vulnerabilities. Insight’s services also encompass cloud security and endpoint protection, ensuring 
that data and devices remain secure across all digital environments.  
 
By integrating these solutions with advanced threat intelligence, Insight helps businesses stay 
ahead of cyberattacks while ensuring compliance and maintaining operational efficiency

Insight Public Sector, Inc. Service Hourly Rates 
Insight’s digital security services empower businesses to protect their data, infrastructure, and users from 
evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity solutions, including 
risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.  
 
Their cybersecurity consulting team works closely with clients to build resilient security strategies tailored 
to specific risks and compliance needs, enabling companies to proactively address vulnerabilities. 
Insight’s services also encompass cloud security and endpoint protection, ensuring that data and devices 
remain secure across all digital environments.

Insight Public Sector, Inc. Service Hourly Rates 
Insight’s digital security services empower businesses to protect their data, infrastructure, and 
users from evolving cyber threats. Our rate catalogue above offers a wide range of cybersecurity 
solutions, including risk assessments, advanced threat detection, and managed security services.  
 
Their cybersecurity consulting team works closely with clients to build resilient security strategies 
tailored to specific risks and compliance needs, enabling companies to proactively address 
vulnerabilities. Insight’s services also encompass cloud security and endpoint protection, ensuring 
that data and devices remain secure across all digital environments.  
 
By integrating these solutions with advanced threat intelligence, Insight helps businesses stay 
ahead of cyberattacks while ensuring compliance and maintaining operational efficiency
